    Loopring ZK-Rollup вҖ” Ethereum L1 Security

    Two Protocols. One Goal.

    Intelligent routing between Loopring and OpenDEX.

    Loopring

    ZK-Rollup

    Non-custodial orderbook on Ethereum L2 with ZK-Proofs for maximum security.

    • ZK-Rollups
    • Ethereum-Level Security
    • Deep Orderbook Liquidity
    • Limit & Stop Orders
    Ideal for: Limit orders, institutional trades

    OpenDEX

    AMM

    UniV2/V3-compatible AMM for instant swaps and liquidity pools on all EVM chains.

    • Instant Token Swaps
    • Multi-Chain Support
    • LP Providing
    • Open-Source (MIT)
    Ideal for: Instant swaps, liquidity providing
